\documentclass[11pt]{article}

    
    
    \usepackage[T1]{fontenc}
    % Nicer default font (+ math font) than Computer Modern for most use cases
    \usepackage{mathpazo}

    % Basic figure setup, for now with no caption control since it's done
    % automatically by Pandoc (which extracts ![](path) syntax from Markdown).
    \usepackage{graphicx}
    % We will generate all images so they have a width \maxwidth. This means
    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.
    \renewcommand{\includegraphics}[1]{\Oldincludegraphics[width=.8\maxwidth]{#1}}
    % Ensure that by default, figures have no caption (until we provide a
    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that
    % in the conversion process - todo).
    \usepackage{caption}
    \DeclareCaptionLabelFormat{nolabel}{}
    \captionsetup{labelformat=nolabel}

    \usepackage{adjustbox} % Used to constrain images to a maximum size 
    \usepackage{xcolor} % Allow colors to be defined
    \usepackage{enumerate} % Needed for markdown enumerations to work
    \usepackage{geometry} % Used to adjust the document margins
    \usepackage{amsmath} % Equations
    \usepackage{amssymb} % Equations
    \usepackage{textcomp} % defines textquotesingle
    % Hack from http://tex.stackexchange.com/a/47451/13684:
    \AtBeginDocument{%
        \def\PYZsq{\textquotesingle}% Upright quotes in Pygmentized code
    }
    \usepackage{upquote} % Upright quotes for verbatim code
    \usepackage{eurosym} % defines \euro
    \usepackage[mathletters]{ucs} % Extended unicode (utf-8) support
    \usepackage[utf8x]{inputenc} % Allow utf-8 characters in the tex document
    \usepackage{fancyvrb} % verbatim replacement that allows latex
    \usepackage{grffile} % extends the file name processing of package graphics 
                         % to support a larger range 
    % The hyperref package gives us a pdf with properly built
    % internal navigation ('pdf bookmarks' for the table of contents,
    % internal cross-reference links, web links for URLs, etc.)
    \usepackage{hyperref}
    \usepackage{longtable} % longtable support required by pandoc >1.10
    \usepackage{booktabs}  % table support for pandoc > 1.12.2
    \usepackage[inline]{enumitem} % IRkernel/repr support (it uses the enumerate* environment)
    \usepackage[normalem]{ulem} % ulem is needed to support strikethroughs (\sout)
                                % normalem makes italics be italics, not underlines

    The form of DAG, \$g\_\{t,t+n\} \$ is \{\(s_t\) : \{\(s_{t+1}\):
\(count \ of \ <s_t, s_{t+1}>\) , ....\}\}

    \subsubsection{Defining the MDP}\label{defining-the-mdp}

the \textbf{state} is \textbf{sequence of games} recent t
\textasciitilde{} t-n bought \[S_t = <g_t> \ \ or\]

\[S_t = <g_{t-1}, g_t>\ \ or\]

\[S_t = <g_{t-2}, g_{t-1}, g_t>\ \ or\]

\[S_t = <g_{t-3},g_{t-2}, g_{t-1}, g_t>\]

the \textbf{action} of MDP correspond to a \textbf{recommendation of an
game} (action 은 game 추천) the \textbf{rewards} of MDP correspond to a
\$r(s\_\{t+1\},a,s\_t)= \{w\_1 \times count( ~\cdot ~,s\_\{t+1\})\} ~ +
~\{w\_2 \times count(s\_\{t+1\}, ~\cdot ~)\} ~, ~~where ~~w\_1 + w\_2 =
1 \$

    transition probability ~
\(tr_{MDP}(<x_1, x_2, x_3>, \ x', \ < x_2, x_3,x''>)\) meaning that
\(P( s_{t+1} \ | \ s_t,a_t)\) ~ \(where\) ~ \$s\_t = \$ , ~ \$s\_\{t+1\}
= \$ , \$a\_t = x' \$ assumptions of initial transition probability

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  A recommendation(action) increases the probability that a user will
  buy an game.

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    This probability is proportional to the probability taht the user
    will buy this game in the absence of recommendation
  \item
    This assumption is made by most CF models dealing with e-commerce
    sites.
  \item
    we denote the proportionality constant by \(\alpha > 1\)
  \end{itemize}
\item
  The probability that a user will buy an game that was not recommened
  is lower than the probability that the agent will buy without
  recommendation.

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    we denote the proportionality constant by \(\beta < 1\)
  \end{itemize}
\end{itemize}

\[tr_{MDP}(<x_1, x_2, x_3>, \ x', \ < x_2, x_3,x'>) = \alpha \cdot tr_{MC}(<x_1, x_2, x_3>, \ < x_2, x_3,x'>) \]

\[tr_{MDP}(<x_1, x_2, x_3>, \ x', \ < x_2, x_3,x''>) = \beta \cdot tr_{MC}(<x_1, x_2, x_3>, \ < x_2, x_3,x''>) \ , \ \  x'' \neq x'\]

\subsubsection{Bellman Equation}\label{bellman-equation}

\[v_\pi(s) = \sum\limits_{a}\pi(a|s)\sum\limits_{s'}tr_{MDP}[r+\gamma v_\pi(s')]\]

                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}action\PYZus{}probList}
                  
              \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{policy\PYZus{}evaluation}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}hash} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{:}\PY{l+m+mf}{0.0} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{state} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}all\PYZus{}states}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}
                  
                  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Bellman Expectation Equation for the every states}
                  \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{state} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}all\PYZus{}states}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{n}{value} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.0}
                      \PY{n}{stateProbList} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}transition\PYZus{}prob\PYZus{}arr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{)}
                      \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{action} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}possibleActions}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                          
                          \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}action\PYZus{}probList} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{copy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{stateProbList}\PY{p}{)}
                          \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}action\PYZus{}probList} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{transition\PYZus{}prob}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{action}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{state\PYZus{}action\PYZus{}probList}\PY{p}{)}
                          \PY{n}{policyProb} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}policy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{action}\PY{p}{]}
                          \PY{n}{reward} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}reward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{action}\PY{p}{)}
                          \PY{n}{nextStates} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{list}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{g\PYZus{}DAG}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{keys}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                          \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}state} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{nextStates}\PY{p}{:}
                              \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}value} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}value}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{next\PYZus{}state}\PY{p}{)}
                              \PY{n}{value} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{policyProb} \PY{o}{*}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{reward} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{state\PYZus{}action\PYZus{}probList}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{state\PYZus{}index}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{next\PYZus{}state}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{*}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{discount\PYZus{}factor} \PY{o}{*} \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}value}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
                      \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}hash}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{value}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}
          
                  \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{value\PYZus{}hash} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}value\PYZus{}hash}
          
              \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{policy\PYZus{}improvement}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}policy} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{policy\PYZus{}hash}
                  \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{state} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}all\PYZus{}states}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{n}{value} \PY{o}{=} \PY{o}{\PYZhy{}}\PY{l+m+mi}{99999}
                      \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}actions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{p}{]}
                      \PY{n}{result} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{\PYZob{}}\PY{p}{\PYZcb{}}  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} initialize the policy}
          
                      \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} for every actions, calculate}
                      \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} [reward + (discount factor) * transition probability*(next state value function)]}
                      \PY{n}{stateProbList} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}transition\PYZus{}prob\PYZus{}arr}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{)}
                      \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{action} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}possibleActions}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}policy}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{action}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.0}
                          \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}state} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{state}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{step}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{action}\PY{p}{)}
                          \PY{n}{reward} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{env}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}reward}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{action}\PY{p}{)}
                          \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}value} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}value}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{next\PYZus{}state}\PY{p}{)}
                          \PY{n}{temp} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{reward} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{discount\PYZus{}factor} \PY{o}{*}\PY{n}{next\PYZus{}value}
          
                          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} We normally can\PYZsq{}t pick multiple actions in greedy policy.}
                          \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} but here we allow multiple actions with same max values}
                          \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{temp} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{value}\PY{p}{:}
                              \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}actions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{action}\PY{p}{)}
                          \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{temp} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{n}{value}\PY{p}{:}
                              \PY{n}{value} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{temp}
                              \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}actions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{clear}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
                              \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}actions}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{action}\PY{p}{)}
          
                      \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} probability of action}
                      \PY{k}{if} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{max\PYZus{}actions}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{!=} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{n}{prob} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mi}{1} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{max\PYZus{}actions}\PY{p}{)}
          
                          \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{actions} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{max\PYZus{}actions}\PY{p}{:}
                              \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}policy}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{actions}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{prob}
          
          
                  \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{policy\PYZus{}table} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{next\PYZus{}policy}
          
              \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} get action according to the current policy}
              \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{get\PYZus{}action}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}pick} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{random}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{randrange}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{100}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{l+m+mi}{100}
          
                  \PY{n}{policy} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{get\PYZus{}policy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{)}
                  \PY{n}{policy\PYZus{}sum} \PY{o}{=} \PY{l+m+mf}{0.0}
                  \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} return the action in the index}
                  \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{index}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{value} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n+nb}{enumerate}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{policy}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                      \PY{n}{policy\PYZus{}sum} \PY{o}{+}\PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{value}
                      \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{random\PYZus{}pick} \PY{o}{\PYZlt{}} \PY{n}{policy\PYZus{}sum}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{index}
          
              \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} get policy of specific state}
              \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{get\PYZus{}policy}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{policy\PYZus{}hash}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{]}

                  \PY{k}{return} \PY{n+nb}{round}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb+bp}{self}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{value\PYZus{}hash}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{state}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+m+mi}{2}\PY{p}{)}

                          \PY{n}{record\PYZus{}sucess\PYZus{}fail}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
                      \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                          \PY{n}{record\PYZus{}sucess\PYZus{}fail}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)}
              \PY{n}{scores}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{append}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{record\PYZus{}sucess\PYZus{}fail}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{/}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{record\PYZus{}sucess\PYZus{}fail}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}
